sin(a + b) = sina * cosb + cosa * sinb
sin(a - b) = sina * cosb - cosa * sinb
cos(a + b) = cosa * cosb - sina * sinb
cos(a - b) = cosa * cosb + sina * sinb ^rj6JLKRI

cos(a + b) = x' / r ^DZ4BMEc0

sin(a + b) = y' / r ^w0hBJPEL

x' = r * cos(a + b) ^lsdxNHrb

cos(a + b) = cosa * cosb - sina * sinb ^Y3tJeoV1

x' = r * (cosa * cosb - sina * sinb) ^MiT4xQ6Y

x' = r * cosa * cosb - r * sina * sinb ^Yw9OYamw

x' = x * cosb - y * sinb ^tHzHG2NB

cosa = x / r ^aZLUbkOp

sina = y / r ^5I50VPST

y' = x * sinb + y * cosb ^XS2LxVlh

同理 ^qAS5Cu8X
